        "## The DARPA TIMIT Acoustic-Phonetic Continuous Speech Corpus (TIMIT)\n",
        "The TIMIT corpus of reading speech has been designed to provide speech data for the acquisition of acoustic-phonetic knowledge and for the development and evaluation of automatic speech recognition systems.\n",
        "\n",
        "This homework is a multiclass classification task, \n",
        "we are going to train a deep neural network classifier to predict the phonemes for each frame from the speech corpus TIMIT.\n",

      "source": [
        "## Create Dataset"
      ]
    },
    {
      "cell_type": "code",
      "metadata": {
        "id": "Fjf5EcmJtf4e"
      },
      "source": [
        "import torch\n",
        "from torch.utils.data import Dataset\n",
        "\n",
        "class TIMITDataset(Dataset):\n",
        "    def __init__(self, X, y=None):\n",
        "        self.data = torch.from_numpy(X).float()\n",
        "        self.data = self.data.view(-1,11,39) #reshape to 2D data (11*39)\n",
        "        print(self.data.shape)\n",
        "        if y is not None:\n",
        "            y = y.astype(np.int)\n",
        "            self.label = torch.LongTensor(y)\n",
        "        else:\n",
        "            self.label = None\n",
        "\n",
        "    def __getitem__(self, idx):\n",
        "        if self.label is not None:\n",
        "            return self.data[idx], self.label[idx]\n",
        "        else:\n",
        "            return self.data[idx]\n",
        "\n",
        "    def __len__(self):\n",
        "        return len(self.data)\n"
      ],
      "execution_count": 3,
      "outputs": []
    },
    {
      "cell_type": "markdown",
      "metadata": {
        "id": "otIC6WhGeh9v"
      },
      "source": [
        "Split the labeled data into a training set and a validation set, you can modify the variable `VAL_RATIO` to change the ratio of validation data."
      ]
    },
    {
      "cell_type": "code",
      "metadata": {
        "id": "sYqi_lAuvC59",
        "colab": {
          "base_uri": "https://localhost:8080/"
        },
        "outputId": "7fec650d-bd49-43d4-b5d2-e1e332b39912"
      },
      "source": [
        "VAL_RATIO = 0.01\n",
        "\n",
        "percent = int(train.shape[0] * (1 - VAL_RATIO))\n",
        "train_x, train_y, val_x, val_y = train[:percent], train_label[:percent], train[percent:], train_label[percent:]\n",
        "print('Size of training set: {}'.format(train_x.shape))\n",
        "print('Size of validation set: {}'.format(val_x.shape))"
      ],
      "execution_count": 4,

      "cell_type": "code",

        "BATCH_SIZE = 100 #set batch = 100\n",
        "\n",
        "from torch.utils.data import DataLoader\n",
        "\n",
        "train_set = TIMITDataset(train_x, train_y)\n",
        "val_set = TIMITDataset(val_x, val_y)\n",
        "train_loader = DataLoader(train_set, batch_size=BATCH_SIZE, shuffle=True) #only shuffle the training data\n",
        "val_loader = DataLoader(val_set, batch_size=BATCH_SIZE, shuffle=False)"
      ],

      "source": [
        "## Create Model"
      ]
    },
    {
      "cell_type": "markdown",
      "metadata": {
        "id": "FYr1ng5fh9pA"
      },
      "source": [
        "Define model architecture, you are encouraged to change and experiment with the model architecture."
      ]
    },
    {
      "cell_type": "code",
      "metadata": {
        "id": "lbZrwT6Ny0XL"
      },
      "source": [
        "import torch\n",
        "import torch.nn as nn\n",
        "import torch.nn.functional as F\n",
        "\n",
        "class Classifier(nn.Module):\n",
        "    def __init__(self):\n",
        "        super(Classifier, self).__init__()\n",
        "        self.layer1 = nn.Sequential(\n",
        "            nn.Linear(39,150),\n",
        "            nn.LayerNorm((11,150)),\n",
        "            nn.ReLU(),\n",
        "            nn.Dropout(p=0.23,inplace=False),\n",
        "        )\n",
        "\n",
        "        self.layer2 = nn.Sequential(\n",
        "            nn.Linear(150,70),\n",
        "            nn.LayerNorm((11,70)),\n",
        "            nn.ReLU(),\n",
        "            nn.Dropout(p=0.2,inplace=False),\n",
        "        )\n",
        "        #two 2D layers\n",
        "        #reference:https://www.cnblogs.com/wanghui-garcia/p/10877700.html\n",
        "        self.flatten = nn.Flatten() #flatten the data to 2D\n",
        "        \n",
        "        self.layer3 = nn.Sequential(\n",
        "            nn.Linear(11*70,1400),\n",
        "            nn.BatchNorm1d(1400),\n",
        "            nn.ReLU(),\n",
        "            nn.Dropout(p=0.24,inplace=False),\n",
        "        )\n",
        "\n",
        "        self.layer4 = nn.Sequential(\n",
        "            nn.Linear(1400,1100),\n",
        "            nn.BatchNorm1d(1100),\n",
        "            nn.ReLU(),\n",
        "            nn.Dropout(p=0.21,inplace=False),\n",
        "        )\n",
        "\n",
        "        self.layer5 = nn.Sequential(\n",
        "            nn.Linear(1100,600),\n",
        "            nn.BatchNorm1d(600),\n",
        "            nn.ReLU(),\n",
        "            nn.Dropout(p=0.2,inplace=False),\n",
        "        )\n",
        "\n",
        "        self.layer6 = nn.Sequential(\n",
        "            nn.Linear(600,350),\n",
        "            nn.BatchNorm1d(350),\n",
        "            nn.ReLU(),\n",
        "            nn.Dropout(p=0.18,inplace=False),\n",
        "        )\n",
        "\n",
        "        self.layer7 = nn.Sequential(\n",
        "            nn.Linear(350,100),\n",
        "            nn.BatchNorm1d(100),\n",
        "            nn.ReLU(),\n",
        "            nn.Dropout(p=0.16,inplace=False),\n",
        "        )\n",
        "\n",
        "        self.out = nn.Linear(100, 39)\n",
        "        self.batchnorm8 = nn.BatchNorm1d(39) \n",
        "        #5 1D layers and 1 outlayers\n",
        "    def forward(self, x):\n",
        "        x = self.layer1(x)     \n",
        "        x = self.layer2(x)\n",
        "\n",
        "        x = self.flatten(x)\n",
        "\n",
        "        x = self.layer3(x)\n",
        "        x = self.layer4(x)\n",
        "        x = self.layer5(x)\n",
        "        x = self.layer6(x)\n",
        "        x = self.layer7(x)\n",
        "\n",
        "        x = self.out(x)\n",
        "        x = self.batchnorm8(x)\n",
        "\n",
        "        return x"
      ],
      "execution_count": 15,
      "outputs": []
    },
    {
      "cell_type": "markdown",
      "metadata": {
        "id": "VRYciXZvPbYh"

        "#check device\n",
        "def get_device():\n",
        "  return 'cuda' if torch.cuda.is_available() else 'cpu'"
      ],
      "execution_count": 16,
      "outputs": []

      "cell_type": "markdown",

      },
      "source": [
        "Fix random seeds for reproducibility."
      ]
    },
    {
      "cell_type": "code",
      "metadata": {
        "id": "88xPiUnm0tAd"
      },
      "source": [
        "# fix random seed\n",
        "def same_seeds(seed):\n",
        "    torch.manual_seed(seed)\n",
        "    if torch.cuda.is_available():\n",
        "        torch.cuda.manual_seed(seed)\n",
        "        torch.cuda.manual_seed_all(seed)  \n",
        "    np.random.seed(seed)  \n",
        "    torch.backends.cudnn.benchmark = False\n",
        "    torch.backends.cudnn.deterministic = True"
      ],
      "execution_count": 17,
      "outputs": []

      "source": [
        "from torchensemble import VotingClassifier\n",
        "# fix random seed for reproducibility\n",
        "same_seeds(0)\n",
        "\n",
        "# get device \n",
        "device = get_device()\n",
        "print(f'DEVICE: {device}')\n",
        "\n",
        "# the path where checkpoint saved\n",
        "model_path = './model.ckpt'\n",
        "\n",
        "# create model, define a loss function, and optimizer\n",
        "model = VotingClassifier(estimator=Classifier,n_estimators=7,cuda=True).to(device) #reference https://github.com/xuyxu/Ensemble-Pytorch\n",
        "criterion = nn.CrossEntropyLoss() \n",
        "model.set_optimizer(\"Adagrad\",lr=0.01,weight_decay=1e-03) #Use Adagrad optimizer"
      ],
